     1→/**
     2→ * AIEngine.js — LLM-driven decision engine.
     3→ *
     4→ * When `endpoint` is null (default) the engine is disabled and characters
     5→ * fall back to random wander controlled by SimulationEngine.
     6→ *
     7→ * To enable, pass an endpoint URL and optionally an API key:
     8→ *   new AIEngine({ endpoint: 'https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', apiKey: '...' })
     9→ *
    10→ * The engine polls each character independently on a configurable interval.
    11→ * Responses are expected as JSON with this shape:
    12→ *   { "action": "move|interact|idle|talk",
    13→ *     "targetId": "object_id",               // for interact
    14→ *     "targetTile": { "tx": 5, "ty": 9 },    // for move
    15→ *     "targetCharacter": "character_name",   // for talk
    16→ *     "dialogue": "optional speech",
    17→ *     "targetDialogue": "response from target character", // for talk
    18→ *     "description": "what the character is doing" }
    19→ */
    20→
    21→export class AIEngine {
    22→  /**
    23→   * @param {object}  [config]
    24→   * @param {string}  [config.endpoint]            - full URL of LLM API endpoint
    25→   * @param {string}  [config.apiKey]              - bearer token / API key
    26→   * @param {string}  [config.model]               - model ID (for Anthropic-style APIs)
    27→   * @param {number}  [config.decisionIntervalMs]  - ms between decisions per char (default 30 000)
    28→   */
    29→  constructor(config = {}) {
    30→    this.endpoint           = config.endpoint           || null;
    31→    this.apiKey             = config.apiKey             || null;
    32→    this.model              = config.model              || 'claude-sonnet-4-6';
    33→    this.decisionIntervalMs = config.decisionIntervalMs || 30_000;
    34→    this.onDecision         = config.onDecision         || null;
    35→
    36→    this.enabled = !!this.endpoint;
    37→
    38→    // Per-character countdown timers  { name → ms until next decision }
    39→    this._timers = new Map();
    40→    // Prevent overlapping requests  { name → true }
    41→    this._pending = new Set();
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  // ── Called by SimulationEngine each frame ─────────────────────────────────
    45→
    46→  update(deltaMs, characters, objects, simState) {
    47→    if (!this.enabled) return;
    48→
    49→    for (const char of characters) {
    50→      let t = this._timers.get(char.name) ?? 0;
    51→      t -= deltaMs;
    52→
    53→      // Don't make decisions while character is held at an object or in conversation;
    54→      // let the timer keep ticking so the cooldown UI stays accurate.
    55→      if (t <= 0 && !this._pending.has(char.name) && char.action !== 'interacting' && char.action !== 'talking') {
    56→        this._timers.set(char.name, this.decisionIntervalMs);
    57→        this._requestDecision(char, characters, objects, simState);
    58→      } else {
    59→        this._timers.set(char.name, t);
    60→      }
    61→    }
    62→  }
    63→
    64→  // ── Internal ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    65→
    66→  async _requestDecision(character, characters, objects, simState) {
    67→    this._pending.add(character.name);
    68→
    69→    try {
    70→      const nearbyObjects = objects
    71→        .filter(obj => {
    72→          const dx = obj.tx - character.tx;
    73→          const dy = obj.ty - character.ty;
    74→          return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= 8;
    75→        })
    76→        .map(o => {
    77→          const slot = o.getSlotInfo();
    78→          // Resolve reserved/occupied character names → display labels for LLM context
    79→          const reservedBy = (o.getReservations?.() ?? [])
    80→            .map(n => characters.find(c => c.name === n)?.label ?? n);
    81→          const occupiedBy = (o.getOccupants?.() ?? [])
    82→            .map(n => characters.find(c => c.name === n)?.label ?? n);
    83→          return {
    84→            id:         o.id,
    85→            label:      o.label,
    86→            state:      o.state,
    87→            slots:      `${slot.available}/${slot.capacity} available`,
    88→            available:  slot.available > 0,
    89→            // Blackboard: show who is already heading here or using it
    90→            intendedBy: reservedBy,
    91→            usedBy:     occupiedBy,
    92→          };
    93→        });
    94→
    95→      const nearbyCharacters = characters
    96→        .filter(c => {
    97→          if (c.name === character.name) return false;
    98→          const dx = c.tx - character.tx;
    99→          const dy = c.ty - character.ty;
   100→          return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= 8;
   101→        })
   102→        .map(c => ({ label: c.label, tx: Math.round(c.tx), ty: Math.round(c.ty), action: c.action }));
   103→
   104→      const systemPrompt =
   105→        `You are ${character.label}, a character in a cosy Japanese home simulation. ` +
   106→        `Decide what to do next based on your mood (${character.mood}/100) and energy (${character.energy}/100). ` +
   107→        `Reply ONLY with valid JSON — no markdown fences, no extra text.`;
   108→
   109→      const userPrompt =
   110→        `Sim time: ${simState.timeString}. ` +
   111→        `You are at tile (${Math.round(character.tx)}, ${Math.round(character.ty)}). ` +
   112→        `Current action: ${character.action}. ` +
   113→        `Nearby objects: ${JSON.stringify(nearbyObjects)}. ` +
   114→        `Nearby characters: ${JSON.stringify(nearbyCharacters)}. ` +
   115→        `Choose one action:
` +
   116→        `  { "action": "move",     "targetTile": {"tx": N, "ty": N}, "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   117→        `  { "action": "interact", "targetId": "object_id",          "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   118→        `  { "action": "idle",                                        "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   119→        `  { "action": "talk",     "targetCharacter": "character_label", "dialogue": "what you say", "targetDialogue": "their response", "description": "..." }`;
   120→
   121→      const headers = { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' };
   122→
   123→      // Build body — compatible with Anthropic Messages API shape by default;
   124→      // swap for OpenAI chat completions if needed by changing endpoint.
   125→      const body = JSON.stringify({
   126→        model: this.model,
   127→        max_tokens: 256,
   128→        system: systemPrompt,
   129→        messages: [{ role: 'user', content: userPrompt }],
   130→      });
   131→
   132→      const res = await fetch(this.endpoint, { method: 'POST', headers, body });
   133→
   134→      if (!res.ok) {
   135→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: HTTP ${res.status}`);
   136→        return;
   137→      }
   138→
   139→      const data = await res.json();
   140→
   141→      // Extract text from Anthropic-style response; fall back to OpenAI style
   142→      let text = data?.content?.[0]?.text     // Anthropic
   143→              ?? data?.choices?.[0]?.message?.content // OpenAI
   144→              ?? null;
   145→
   146→      if (!text) {
   147→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: unrecognised response shape`, data);
   148→        return;
   149→      }
   150→
   151→      const decision = JSON.parse(text);
   152→      this._applyDecision(character, decision, characters, objects, simState);
   153→    } catch (err) {
   154→      console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}:`, err);
   155→    } finally {
   156→      this._pending.delete(character.name);
   157→    }
   158→  }
   159→
   160→  _applyDecision(character, decision, characters, objects, simState) {
   161→    if (!decision?.action) return;
   162→
   163→    switch (decision.action) {
   164→      case 'move':
   165→        if (decision.targetTile) {
   166→          // Release any pending object reservation before moving freely
   167→          if (character.targetObjectId) {
   168→            const prevObj = objects.find(o => o.id === character.targetObjectId);
   169→            if (prevObj) {
   170→              prevObj.release(character.name);
   171→              if (simState?.pushEvent) {
   172→                simState.pushEvent({
   173→                  type:      'fallback',
   174→                  charLabel: character.label,
   175→                  reason:    'plan_changed',
   176→                  fromLabel: prevObj.label ?? prevObj.name,
   177→                  toLabel:   null,
   178→                });
   179→              }
   180→            }
   181→            character.targetObjectId = null;
   182→          }
   183→          character.moveTo(decision.targetTile.tx, decision.targetTile.ty);
   184→        }
   185→        break;
   186→
   187→      case 'interact': {
   188→        const obj = objects.find(o => o.id === decision.targetId);
   189→        if (obj) {
   190→          // If already heading to a different object, release that reservation first
   191→          let abandonedLabel = null;
   192→          if (character.targetObjectId && character.targetObjectId !== obj.id) {
   193→            const prevObj = objects.find(o => o.id === character.targetObjectId);
   194→            if (prevObj) {
   195→              prevObj.release(character.name);
   196→              abandonedLabel = prevObj.label ?? prevObj.name;
   197→            }
   198→            character.targetObjectId = null;
   199→          }
   200→
   201→          // Only commit if a slot is available and object is currently interactable
   202→          const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   203→          if (!obj.isFull() && stateDef?.transitions?.use) {
   204→            // Walk to an adjacent walkable tile (same pattern as wander engine)
   205→            const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   206→            if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   207→              if (obj.reserve(character.name)) { // claim slot; guard against any race
   208→                character.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   209→                character.pendingAction  = 'use';
   210→                if (abandonedLabel && simState?.pushEvent) {
   211→                  simState.pushEvent({
   212→                    type:      'fallback',
   213→                    charLabel: character.label,
   214→                    reason:    'plan_changed',
   215→                    fromLabel: abandonedLabel,
   216→                    toLabel:   obj.label ?? obj.name,
   217→                  });
   218→                }
   219→              }
   220→            }
   221→          } else if (abandonedLabel && simState?.pushEvent) {
   222→            // New target unavailable — character goes idle after abandoning previous
   223→            simState.pushEvent({
   224→              type:      'fallback',
   225→              charLabel: character.label,
   226→              reason:    'object_unavailable',
   227→              fromLabel: abandonedLabel,
   228→              toLabel:   null,
   229→            });
   230→          }
   231→        }
   232→        break;
   233→      }
   234→
   235→      case 'idle':
   236→        // Release any pending reservation, then stay put for one full decision interval
   237→        if (character.targetObjectId) {
   238→          const prevObj = objects.find(o => o.id === character.targetObjectId);
   239→          if (prevObj) {
   240→            prevObj.release(character.name);
   241→            if (simState?.pushEvent) {
   242→              simState.pushEvent({
   243→                type:      'fallback',
   244→                charLabel: character.label,
   245→                reason:    'plan_changed',
   246→                fromLabel: prevObj.label ?? prevObj.name,
   247→                toLabel:   null,
   248→              });
   249→            }
   250→          }
   251→          character.targetObjectId = null;
   252→        }
   253→        character.wanderTimer = this.decisionIntervalMs;
   254→        break;
   255→
   256→      case 'talk': {
   257→        const target = characters.find(c => c.label === decision.targetCharacter);
   258→        if (target) {
   259→          // Evaluate Phase: check if B can accept a conversation request.
   260→          // Accept if idle or walking; reject if interacting, talking, or otherwise busy.
   261→          const canAccept = target.action === 'idle' || target.action === 'walking';
   262→
   263→          if (!canAccept) {
   264→            // B is busy — log the rejection and let A fall back to idle/wander
   265→            if (simState?.pushEvent) {
   266→              simState.pushEvent({
   267→                type:           'talk_rejected',
   268→                initiatorLabel: character.label,
   269→                targetLabel:    target.label,
   270→                reason:         target.action,
   271→              });
   272→            }
   273→            // A idles for the normal decision interval (fallback handled by Engine wander)
   274→            character.wanderTimer = this.decisionIntervalMs;
   275→            break;
   276→          }
   277→
   278→          // Release any previous object reservation before walking to talk
   279→          if (character.targetObjectId) {
   280→            const prevObj = objects.find(o => o.id === character.targetObjectId);
   281→            if (prevObj) {
   282→              prevObj.release(character.name);
   283→              if (simState?.pushEvent) {
   284→                simState.pushEvent({
   285→                  type:      'fallback',
   286→                  charLabel: character.label,
   287→                  reason:    'plan_changed',
   288→                  fromLabel: prevObj.label ?? prevObj.name,
   289→                  toLabel:   target.label,
   290→                });
   291→              }
   292→            }
   293→            character.targetObjectId = null;
   294→          }
   295→
   296→          // Request Phase: walk A to a tile adjacent to B.
   297→          // Arrival handler in Engine will start the shared talking state.
   298→          const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty));
   299→          if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   300→            // Store pending talk so Engine knows what to do on arrival
   301→            character.pendingTalkTarget   = target;
   302→            character.pendingTalkDialogue = decision.dialogue       || null;
   303→            character.pendingTalkResponse = decision.targetDialogue || null;
   304→          }
   305→        }
   306→        break;
   307→      }
   308→    }
   309→
   310→    // For talk actions, dialogue is held until both characters enter talking state.
   311→    if (decision.dialogue && decision.action !== 'talk') {
   312→      character.currentDialogue = decision.dialogue;
   313→      character.dialogueTimer   = 5000;
   314→    }
   315→
   316→    if (decision.description) {
   317→      console.log(`[${character.label}] ${decision.description}`);
   318→    }
   319→
   320→    if (this.onDecision) {
   321→      this.onDecision(character, decision, objects, simState);
   322→    }
   323→  }
   324→}
   325→

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #49
Now I have a clear picture. Let me plan the fix: The main issue is that the LLM receives `nearbyCharacters` with their `action` states, but doesn't get any explicit guidance to only select idle/walking characters for talk targets. Additionally, there's LLM bias toward Maple. The fix has two parts: 1. **Filter busy characters from talk targets in the prompt** - Separate the `nearbyCharacters` data into idle/walking targets and a separate list of busy ones, OR more directly, add clear guidance in the prompt that says "For talk action, only choose characters with action idle or walking" 2. **Add explicit prompt guidance** about when to use talk I'm leaning toward a two-pronged approach: add an `available` flag to the character data that marks whether they're idle or walking, then reinforce this in the prompt with clear instructions that talk targets must be available. I'm leaning toward filtering unavailable characters entirely from the talk target list, since that's more reliable than relying on the LLM to follow instructions—though I should keep them visible for other purposes so the LLM doesn't get confused about characters it knows exist. The cleanest solution is adding a `canTalk` boolean to each character and explicitly stating in the prompt that only characters with `canTalk: true` can be talk targets, which gives the LLM both the data and clear guidance. This filtering approach should also help address the bias toward targeting Maple for every talk attempt. Building the character filtering logic... I'm reconsidering the approach—should I add a `canTalk` property check or filter busy characters server-side instead? The issue suggests doing both: filtering out idle/walking characters in the prompt guidance and also filtering them engine-side from the talk target list, so I'll implement both strategies to be thorough. that character is no longer nearby. I think Approach 2 is better—it keeps the LLM fully informed about who's around while being explicit about who's actually available to talk to. I see the LLM is already receiving the `action` field but ignoring it when selecting talk targets. The cleanest solution is adding a `canTalk` boolean flag to each nearby character and explicitly instructing the LLM to only initiate conversations with characters where this flag is true. Now I'll create the feature branch and start implementing this fix.

{"id":"fa54503c-6a2b-4090-8c16-5e2afef4520a","identifier":"FRG-228","title":"Bug: Talk action never succeeds — LLM always targets busy character","description":"## Problem

In 14+ sim hours, 4 talk attempts were made — all targeted Maple, who was always interacting. All 4 were REJECTED. Zero successful conversations. The talking state, purple badge, face-each-other, and timer features are completely unverified in production.

## Root Causes

1. **LLM bias:** All talk attempts target Maple. Sol and Nyx never try to talk to each other.
2. **Timing:** Maple is nearly always interacting, so talk requests always get rejected.
3. **No engine-level mitigation:** The engine presents all nearby characters as talk targets but doesn't indicate their availability in the prompt.

## Fix Options

1. Include character availability in the LLM prompt context (e.g., action: idle vs action: interacting) — already sent but LLM ignores it
2. Add prompt guidance: 'Only choose talk if the target character is idle or walking'
3. Engine-side: filter out busy characters from the talk target list in the prompt
4. Increase talk likelihood: add prompt hint encouraging conversation

## Acceptance Criteria

* At least 1 successful talk observed per \\~2 sim hours
